## 进(進)入( )
---
## enter; get into
### jìnrù
---
- **traditional:** 進入
- **definition:** enter; get into
- **pinyin:** jìnrù
- **components:**
  - 进(進)
    - jìn
    - advance; move forward
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter; join; get into; go in
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 進 (jìn, "advance") conveys moving forward or ahead, suggesting motion or progression into something. 入 (rù, "enter") directly means to step into or become part of a space or realm, conveying entry.
  - **interpretation:** 進 (jìn, "advance") implies moving forward towards a destination. 入 (rù, "enter") suggests completing the motion of crossing a boundary into a new space. Combine these to express the idea of 'entering' as moving forward into a space or state.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)进(進)入( )公( )园(園)。
    - Wǒmen jìnrù gōngyuán.
    - We entered the park.
  - 请(請)在( )进(進)入( )房( )间(間)前( )脱(脫)鞋( )。
    - Qǐng zài jìnrù fángjiān qián tuōxié.
    - Please remove your shoes before entering the room.
  - 他( )进(進)入( )大( )学(學)后(後)学(學)习(習)很( )勤( )奋(奮)。
    - Tā jìnrù dàxué hòu xuéxí hěn qínfèn.
    - He studied diligently after entering the university.
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進)
- **traditional:** 進
- **definition:** advance; move forward
- **pinyin:** jìn
- **components:**
  - 辵
    - chuò
    - walk; movement
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tail bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 辵 ('walk/movement') + 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tail bird') =
    - a bird that can only move forward
  - **interpretation:** The character 進 (jìn, 'to advance') combines the idea of movement with the imagery of a bird, symbolizing forward movement, as the bird naturally progresses forward on foot.
  - **simplification:** 進 was simplified to 进(進) by replacing the phonetic component 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tail bird') with 井 (jǐng, 'well') to reduce strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )决(決)定( )继(繼)续(續)努( )力( )，以( )便( )在( )职(職)业(業)生( )涯( )中( )进(進)步( )。
    - Tā juédìng jìxù nǔlì, yǐbiàn zài zhíyè shēngyá zhōng jìnbù.
    - He decided to keep working hard in order to advance in his career.
  - 在( )我( )们(們)进(進)入( )隧( )道( )时(時)，速( )度( )变(變)得( )越( )来(來)越( )快( )。
    - Zài wǒmen jìnrù suìdào shí, sùdù biàn de yuè lái yuè kuài.
    - As we entered the tunnel, the speed became faster and faster.
  - 大( )门(門)刚(剛)一( )打( )开(開)，他( )就( )立( )刻( )走( )了( )进(進)去( )。
    - Dàmén gāng yī dǎkāi, tā jiù lìkè zǒu le jìnqù.
    - As soon as the door opened, he immediately walked in.
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵
- **definition:** walk; movement
- **pinyin:** chuò
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - walk
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 彳 (chì, "walk") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop") ->
    - 𣥆 ->
    - stylized as 龰 ->
    - 辵
  - **interpretation:** The character 辵 combines 彳 (chì, "walk"), which represents movement, with 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop"), suggesting the concept of stepping or traveling forward. This character represents the idea of movement, particularly the action of walking or traveling, as originally depicted by the more conservative form 𣥆. Over time, the bottom component has been stylized as 龰, forming the current representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )辵( )在( )乡(鄉)间(間)的( )小( )路( )上( )。
    - Tā chuò zài xiāngjiān de xiǎolù shàng.
    - He walks on the rural path.
  - 晨( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )，他( )辵( )出( )门(門)开(開)始( )旅( )程( )。
    - Chén guāng sǎ mǎn dàdì, tā chuò chūmén kāishǐ lǚchéng.
    - As the morning light fills the earth, he sets out to begin his journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辵](@media/glyph8fb5.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 彳
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** chì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a foot or person walking
  - **interpretation:** 彳(chì, 'walking') visually represents steps or a person moving, suggesting the idea of walking or movement. Despite a simplified history from characters like 行(xíng, 'walk'), its pictographic heritage directly connects with the notion of stepping or proceeding.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )河( )边(邊)慢( )慢( )地( )走( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài hé biān mànmàn de zǒu.
    - He likes to walk slowly by the river.
  - 我( )们(們)每( )天( )退( )出( )喧( )嚣(囂)，享( )受( )安( )静(靜)的( )散( )步( )。
    - Wǒmen měitiān tuìchū xuānxiāo, xiǎngshòu ānjìng de sànbù.
    - We withdraw from the hustle and bustle every day to enjoy a quiet walk.
  - 他( )常( )常( )独(獨)自( )彳( )亍( )于(於)公( )园(園)小( )径(徑)。
    - Tā chángcháng dúzì chìchù yú gōngyuán xiǎojìng.
    - He often walks alone on the park trails.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 彳](@media/glyph5f73.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他( )走( )路( )时(時)小( )心( )谨(謹)慎( )，因( )为(爲)止( )若( )受( )伤(傷)便( )难(難)前( )行( )。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )受( )伤(傷)了( )。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她( )用( )脚(腳)趾( )轻(輕)轻(輕)地( )踢( )了( )一( )下( )球( )。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在( )沙( )滩(灘)上( )散( )步( )时(時)，我( )感( )受( )到( )沙( )子( )在( )我( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )间(間)流( )动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)后(後)，他( )的( )足( )不( )能( )动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小( )明( )打( )球( )时(時)，不( )小( )心( )扭( )伤(傷)了( )足( )。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我( )每( )天( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足( )部( )。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 隹
- **definition:** short-tail bird
- **pinyin:** zhuī
- **components:**
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a short‐tailed bird (e.g., a sparrow) ->
    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只( )短( )尾( )的( )隹( )在( )树(樹)林( )中( )飞(飛)翔( )。
    - Zhè zhī duǎnwěi de zhuī zài shùlín zhōng fēixiáng.
    - This short-tailed bird flies in the forest.
  - 博( )物( )馆(館)里(裡)展( )出( )了( )一( )件( )以( )隹( )为(為)题(題)材( )的( )古( )代( )绘(繪)画(畫)。
    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古( )诗(詩)篇( )中( )常( )用( )隹( )来(來)象( )征(徵)自( )由( )，寓( )意( )生( )动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.
    - In ancient poems, the short-tailed bird is often used to symbolize freedom, conveying vivid meaning.

### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕
- **definition:** cry of a bird
- **pinyin:** yǎo
- **components:**
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 唯 (phonetic) + 鳥 (semantic, "bird") ->
    - cry of a bird
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 唯 (wéi, used phonetically for its sound) with 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") to denote the specific sound relating to a bird's cry.
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**
  - 唯有努力，才能成功。
    - Wéi yǒu nǔlì, cái néng chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one succeed.

    - Wéi yǒu zài ānjìng de yèwǎn, wǒ cái néng tīng qīng zìjǐ de xīnshēng.
    - Only in the quiet of the night can I hear my own heart.
  - 我( )唯( )爱(愛)读(讀)书(書)，因( )为(為)书(書)籍( )能( )带(帶)给(給)我( )无(無)限( )的( )可( )能( )。
    - Wǒ wéi ài dúshū, yīnwèi shūjí néng dài gěi wǒ wúxiàn de kěnéng.
    - I only love reading, because books bring me infinite possibilities.
- **historical forms:**

### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 进(進)入( ) → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕 → 鳥
- **definition:** bird
- **pinyin:** niǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird with a prominent beak and tail feathers
  - **interpretation:** The character 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") visually represents a bird, featuring distinct elements such as a beak and tail feathers, capturing its essence through its graphical form.
- **examples:**
  - 花( )园(園)里(裡)有( )许(許)多( )鸟(鳥)，在空中翱翔。

    - Shùlín zhōng yǒu yī zhī niǎo, zài zhītóu tiàoyuè.

### 进(進)入( ) → 入
- **definition:** enter; join; get into; go in
- **pinyin:** rù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'
  - **interpretation:** The character 入(rù, 'enter') visually represents the concept of entering, with the form resembling an arrowhead suggesting movement through an opening.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)入( )座( )。
    - Qǐng rùzuò.
    - Please take a seat.
  - 学(學)生( )走( )入( )校( )园(園)，开(開)始( )新( )学(學)期( )。
    - Xuéshēng zǒu rù xiàoyuán, kāishǐ xīn xuéqī.
    - The students enter the campus and start a new semester.
  - 游(遊)客( )走( )入( )古( )城( )，探( )索( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Yóukè zǒu rù gǔchéng, tànsuǒ lìshǐ.
    - The tourists enter the ancient city and explore its history.

## enter; get into

## 梦(夢)
---
## dream
### mèng
---
- **traditional:** 夢
- **definition:** dream
- **pinyin:** mèng
- **components:**
  - 爿
    - pán
    - bed
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 夕
    - xī
    - night
  - 瞢
    - méng
    - bewildered
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Oracle bone script: person 人 (rén, 'person') lying on bed 爿 (pán, 'bed') + eye 目 (mù, 'eye') with emphasis ->
    - Bronze inscriptions: 目 with eyebrows 眉 + person as dots + moon 夕 (xī, 'night') added ->
    - 夢: eyebrows 卝 + eyes 罒 + person's body 冖 + 夕 ->
    - phono-semantic compound: phonetic 瞢 + semantic 夕
  - **interpretation:** In the oracle bone script, 夢 evokes a person on a bed with an emphasized eye, suggesting a state of being where one's vision is active despite resting, which aligns with dreaming. By the Bronze inscriptions, with the addition of 夕, it highlights the nocturnal and unconscious nature of dreams. Modern 夢 combines phonetic 瞢 with semantic 夕, reflecting dreaming as something occurring at night.
  - **simplification:** 梦 is a simplified form of 夢 where 目 + 冖 is simplified to a simpler eye component and 冖.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )昨( )晚( )做( )了( )一( )个(個)美( )好( )的( )梦(夢)。
    - Wǒ zuó wǎn zuò le yī gè měihǎo de mèng.
    - I had a wonderful dream last night.
  - 她( )希( )望( )有( )一( )天( )能( )实(實)现(現)自( )己( )的( )梦(夢)想( )。
    - Tā xīwàng yǒu yī tiān néng shíxiàn zìjǐ de mèngxiǎng.
    - She hopes to fulfill her dreams one day.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )应(應)该(該)追( )寻(尋)自( )己( )的( )梦(夢)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yīnggāi zhuīxún zìjǐ de mèng.
    - Everyone should pursue their own dreams.
### 梦(夢) → 爿
- **definition:** bed
- **pinyin:** pán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "possess")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿 (pán, "bed") visually represents a bed, emphasizing its usage in denoting places for resting or sleeping. It served as the original form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed"), reinforcing its meaning. Additionally, in the character 臧 (zāng, "possess"), it appears as a contracted form, reflecting its historical usage in composite forms.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爿](@media/glyph723f.png)
### 梦(夢) → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 梦(夢) → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她( )目( )不( )转(轉)睛( )，注( )视(視)前( )方( )。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄( )鹰(鷹)展( )翅( )，双(雙)目( )炯( )炯( )看( )天( )际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 梦(夢) → 夕
- **definition:** night
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a moon crescent
  - **interpretation:** The character 夕 (xī, 'evening') is a pictogram that represents a crescent moon, capturing the image of the moon in the evening sky. The comparison to 月 (yuè, 'moon') underscores its depiction of the moon phase commonly associated with evening.
- **examples:**
  - 夕( )阳(陽)西( )下( )。
    - xī yáng xīxià.
    - The setting sun descends.
  - 夕( )阳(陽)西( )下( )，晚( )风(風)徐( )徐( )。
    - xī yáng xīxià, wǎn fēng xúxú.
    - The sun sets as the gentle evening breeze blows.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夕](@media/glyph5915.png)
### 梦(夢) → 夕 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )空( )挂(掛)着(著)明( )月( )。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人( )们(們)赏(賞)月( )，寄( )托(託)相( )思( )。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢
- **definition:** bewildered
- **pinyin:** méng
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - departed; gone; lost
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 目 (mù, "eye") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - sense of being lost or disoriented, particularly in vision ->
    - bewildered
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 目 (mù, "eye") as the semantic component with 亡 (wáng) as the phonetic component, suggesting a state where one's vision is metaphorically lost or confused, reflecting the meaning of being bewildered.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 瞢](@media/glyph77a2.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡
- **definition:** departed; gone; lost
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 芒
    - máng
    - edge of a knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line on 刀 (dāo, 'knife') ->
    - cutting edge of a knife ->
    - original form of 芒 (máng, 'edge of a knife')
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a line on a knife, representing the sharp edge. This connection to sharpness and cutting leads to the concept of 'perish,' as an edge can cut or end something, symbolically indicating destruction or the end of life.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士( )们(們)在( )战(戰)场(場)上( )英( )勇( )战(戰)斗(鬥)，许(許)多( )人( )不( )幸( )亡( )。
    - Zhànshìmen zài zhànchǎng shàng yīngyǒng zhàndòu, xǔduō rén bùxìng wáng.
    - The soldiers fought bravely on the battlefield, and many unfortunately perished.
  - 如( )果( )不( )努( )力( )经(經)营(營)，这(這)家( )公( )司( )可( )能( )会(會)亡( )。
    - Rúguǒ bù nǔlì jīngyíng, zhè jiā gōngsī kěnéng huì wáng.
    - If the company does not operate diligently, it may perish.
  - 古( )代( )帝( )国(國)由( )于(於)内(內)外( )问(問)题(題)而( )一( )朝( )亡( )。
    - Gǔdài dìguó yóuyú nèiwài wèntí ér yī zhāo wáng.
    - The ancient empire perished overnight due to internal and external issues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亡](@media/glyph4ea1.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )锋(鋒)利( )的( )刀( )，切( )开(開)蔬( )菜( )。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把( )刀( )非( )常( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小( )心( )地( )持( )刀( )，为(為)客( )人( )切( )肉( )。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 刀](@media/glyph5200.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒
- **definition:** edge of a knife
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - to flee
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - edge of a knife
  - **interpretation:** The character 芒(máng, "edge of a knife") uses the 艹 (cǎo, "grass") component to highlight its relation to plant life or natural elements, while 亡 (wáng) provides the phonetic indication. Originally it may have depicted something like 方 but evolved to illustrate the thinness or sharpness of grass edges, metaphorically linking to the sharp edge of a knife.
- **examples:**
  - 刀( )的( )芒( )在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光( )。
    - Dāo de máng zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The edge of the knife glistens in the sunlight.
  - 我( )们(們)要( )小( )心( )刀( )的( )芒( )，因( )为(為)它( )非( )常( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - Wǒmen yào xiǎoxīn dāo de máng, yīnwèi tā fēicháng fēnglì.
    - We must be careful of the knife's edge because it is very sharp.
  - 他( )用( )手( )指( )轻(輕)轻(輕)触(觸)摸( )刀( )的( )芒( )，感( )受( )到( )它( )的( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ qīngqīng chùmō dāo de máng, gǎnshòudào tā de fēnglì.
    - He gently touched the blade's edge with his finger and felt its sharpness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 芒](@media/glyph8292.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )写(寫)字( )时(時)用( )艹( )作( )草( )字( )的( )偏( )旁( )。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春( )天( )到( )来(來)时(時)，艹( )生( )长(長)得( )很( )快( )。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.

## 一生
---
## all one's life; a lifetime
### yìshēng
---
- **definition:** all one's life; a lifetime
- **pinyin:** yìshēng
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single; whole
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life; birth; alive; grow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 一 (yī, "one") indicates a singularity or unity, while 生 (shēng, "life") signifies the concept of living or existence. Combined, they refer to everything from birth to death, encapsulating a complete span of life.
  - **interpretation:** The word 一生 (yìshēng) portrays the idea of a single, complete life journey. 一 (yī, "one") emphasizes the entirety or singularity of one's existence, while 生 (shēng, "life") denotes the period of living from birth to death. Together, they convey the notion of an individual's entire life span.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )一( )生( )都( )在( )追( )求( )梦(夢)想( )。
    - Tā yìshēng dōu zài zhuīqiú mèngxiǎng.
    - He spent all his life chasing dreams.
  - 她( )一( )生( )中( )最( )快( )乐(樂)的( )时(時)光( )是( )和( )家( )人( )在( )一( )起( )。
    - Tā yìshēng zhōng zuì kuàilè de shíguāng shì hé jiārén zài yīqǐ.
    - Her happiest times in life were spent with her family.
  - 老( )师(師)把( )他( )的( )一( )生( )都( )奉( )献(獻)给(給)了( )教( )育( )事( )业(業)。
    - Lǎoshī bǎ tā de yìshēng dōu fèngxiàn gěi le jiàoyù shìyè.
    - The teacher devoted his entire life to the cause of education.
### 一生 → 一
- **definition:** one; single; whole
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 一生 → 生
- **definition:** life; birth; alive; grow
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生( )命( )是( )一( )场(場)美( )丽(麗)的( )旅( )程( )。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他( )在( )战(戰)场(場)上( )奋(奮)力( )生( )存( )。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家( )餐( )厅(廳)的( )生( )鱼(魚)片( )非( )常( )新( )鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 生](@media/glyph751f.png)
### 一生 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)后(後)，小( )屮( )冲(沖)破( )泥( )土( )而( )出( )。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)

## 中
---
## in
### zhōng
---
- **definition:** in
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看( )着(著)远(遠)方( )。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房( )间(間)正( )中( )，挂(掛)着(著)一( )幅( )名( )画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)

## 中

## in

## 难(難)忘( )
---
## unforgettable; memorable
### nánwàng
---
- **traditional:** 難忘
- **definition:** unforgettable; memorable
- **pinyin:** nánwàng
- **components:**
  - 难(難)
    - nán
    - difficult
  - 忘
    - wàng
    - forget
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 難 (nán, "difficult") + 忘 (wàng, "forget") =
    - hard to forget ->
    - unforgettable
  - **interpretation:** The word 難忘 (nánwàng, "unforgettable") combines 難 (nán, "difficult") and 忘 (wàng, "forget") to describe something that leaves a strong impression, making it difficult to erase from memory.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)次( )旅( )行( )非( )常( )难(難)忘( )。
    - Zhè cì lǚxíng fēicháng nánwàng.
    - This trip was unforgettable.
  - 他( )给(給)我( )留( )下( )了( )难(難)忘( )的( )印( )象( )。
    - Tā gěi wǒ liúxiàle nánwàng de yìnxiàng.
    - He left me with an unforgettable impression.
  - 毕(畢)业(業)典( )礼(禮)是( )一( )个(個)难(難)忘( )的( )时(時)刻( )。
    - Bìyè diǎnlǐ shì yīgè nánwàng de shíkè.
    - The graduation ceremony was a memorable moment.
### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難)
- **traditional:** 難
- **definition:** difficult
- **pinyin:** nán
- **components:**
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - bird
  - 暵
    - hàn
    - drought
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 隹 (zhuī, 'bird') + phonetic 暵 (hàn) ->
    - originally depicted a type of bird ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'difficult'
  - **interpretation:** The character 难(難) (nán, 'difficult') combines the semantic component 隹 (zhuī, 'bird') with the phonetic 暵 (hàn). It originally depicted a specific type of bird, but was phonetically borrowed to express 'difficult'. This phonetic borrowing extends the meaning beyond its literal components.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 難 was simplified by eliminating the left component and retaining 又 (yòu, 'again').
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)道( )题(題)很( )难(難)。
    - Zhè dào tí hěn nán.
    - This question is very difficult.
  - 他( )觉(覺)得( )学(學)中( )文( )很( )难(難)，但( )是( )他( )会(會)努( )力( )。
    - Tā juéde xué Zhōngwén hěn nán, dànshì tā huì nǔlì.
    - He thinks learning Chinese is difficult, but he will try hard.
  - 解( )决(決)这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)很( )难(難)，我( )们(們)需( )要( )更( )多( )时(時)间(間)。
    - Jiějué zhège wèntí hěn nán, wǒmen xūyào gèng duō shíjiān.
    - It's difficult to solve this problem, we need more time.
### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 隹

- **pinyin:** zhuī

    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
  - 唯
    - wéi

    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").

    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕
- **definition:** cry of a bird
- **pinyin:** yǎo
- **components:**
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 唯 (phonetic) + 鳥 (semantic, "bird") ->
    - cry of a bird
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 唯 (wéi, used phonetically for its sound) with 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") to denote the specific sound relating to a bird's cry.
### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**

  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。

- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 堇
    - jǐn
    - burnt earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** 日 (rì, "sun") + 堇 (jǐn, phonetic element linked to heat and fire)
  - **interpretation:** The character 暵 (xiàn, "dry") combines the semantic component 日 (rì, "sun"), representing heat from the sun, with the phonetic component 堇 (jǐn), which suggests burning or heat. The combination evokes the sense of intense heat and dryness, as one might experience under a scorching sun.

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 暵 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇
- **definition:** burnt earth
- **pinyin:** jǐn
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
  - 廿
    - niàn
    - twenty
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 大 (person) + 火 (fire) + 廿 (open mouth screaming) =
    - a person being burned in a sacrificial ceremony ->
    - burnt earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 堇(jǐn, "burnt earth") combines the elements of a person 大(dà, "big") depicted as being part of a sacrifice, with 火(huǒ, "fire") representing a burning action. 廿(niàn, "twenty") is stylized here to depict an open mouth screaming, emphasizing the ritual aspect. The fire ritual thus conveys the idea of burnt earth used in sacrificial ceremonies, believed necessary for invoking rain or fertility in ancient practices.

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 大
- **definition:** big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.

  - 此( )夫( )心( )怀(懷)大( )志( )。

### 难(難)忘( ) → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 廿 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )十( )本( )书(書)。

    - I have ten books.

  - 十( )年( )磨( )一( )剑(劍)。

### 难(難)忘( ) → 忘 → 亡 → 芒
- **definition:** edge of a knife
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - to flee
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - edge of a knife
  - **interpretation:** The character 芒(máng, "edge of a knife") uses the 艹 (cǎo, "grass") component to highlight its relation to plant life or natural elements, while 亡 (wáng) provides the phonetic indication. Originally it may have depicted something like 方 but evolved to illustrate the thinness or sharpness of grass edges, metaphorically linking to the sharp edge of a knife.
- **examples:**
  - 刀( )的( )芒( )在( )阳(陽)光( )下( )闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光( )。
    - Dāo de máng zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The edge of the knife glistens in the sunlight.
  - 我( )们(們)要( )小( )心( )刀( )的( )芒( )，因( )为(為)它( )非( )常( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - Wǒmen yào xiǎoxīn dāo de máng, yīnwèi tā fēicháng fēnglì.
    - We must be careful of the knife's edge because it is very sharp.
  - 他( )用( )手( )指( )轻(輕)轻(輕)触(觸)摸( )刀( )的( )芒( )，感( )受( )到( )它( )的( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ qīngqīng chùmō dāo de máng, gǎnshòudào tā de fēnglì.
    - He gently touched the blade's edge with his finger and felt its sharpness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 芒](@media/glyph8292.png)
### 难(難)忘( ) → 忘 → 亡 → 芒 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )写(寫)字( )时(時)用( )艹( )作( )草( )字( )的( )偏( )旁( )。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春( )天( )到( )来(來)时(時)，艹( )生( )长(長)得( )很( )快( )。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 难(難)忘( ) → 忘 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一( )直( )都( )在( )帮(幫)助( )别(別)人( )。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有( )一( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )公( )园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多( )人( )来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.
- **historical forms:**

## 老年
---
## old age
### lǎonián
---
- **definition:** old age
- **pinyin:** lǎonián
- **components:**
  - 老
    - lǎo
    - old; venerable; experienced
  - 年
    - nián
    - year; age
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 老 (lǎo, "old") refers to age or elderliness, and 年 (nián, "year") refers to the concept of time or age in years. Together, 老年 specifically denotes the period of life known as old age.
  - **interpretation:** 老 (lǎo, "old") indicates a stage in life characterized by experience and wisdom accumulated over time. 年 (nián, "year") brings in the temporal aspect, emphasizing the cumulative passage of years. Thus, 老年 represents the accumulation of years in life, focusing on the advanced age stage, often associated with retirement and reflection.
- **examples:**
  - 在老年，保持健康是非常重要的。
    - Zài lǎonián, bǎochí jiànkāng shì fēicháng zhòngyào de.
    - In old age, maintaining health is very important.
  - 他的老年生活很幸福。
    - Tā de lǎonián shēnghuó hěn xìngfú.
    - His old age is very happy.
  - 人( )们(們)常( )常( )在( )老( )年( )时(時)回( )忆(憶)过(過)去( )。
    - Rénmen chángcháng zài lǎonián shí huíyì guòqù.
    - People often recall the past in old age.
### 老年 → 老
- **definition:** old; venerable; experienced
- **pinyin:** lǎo
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - man
  - 毛
    - máo
    - hair
  - 匕
    - bǐ
    - cane
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "man") + 毛 (máo, "hair") + 匕 (bǐ, "cane") =
    - a man with long hair leaning on a cane ->
    - old man
  - **interpretation:** The character 老(lǎo) visually depicts aspects associated with age: a man with long hair and a cane. This combination intuitively suggests the concept of being elderly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )虽(雖)然( )年( )老( )，但( )经(經)验(驗)丰(豐)富( )。
    - tā suīrán niánlǎo, dàn jīngyàn fēngfù.
    - He may be old, but he is experienced.
  - 他( )是( )我( )们(們)班( )的( )老( )老( )师(師)。
    - tā shì wǒmen bān de lǎo lǎoshī.
    - He is our class's venerable teacher.
  - 老( )故( )事( )传(傳)递(遞)智( )慧( )。
    - lǎo gùshi chuándì zhìhuì.
    - Old stories convey wisdom.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 老](@media/glyph8001.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 人
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 毛
- **definition:** hair
- **pinyin:** máo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a feather or hair
  - **interpretation:** The character 毛(máo, "hair") visually represents either a feather or the strands of hair, capturing the texture and common features of these natural elements.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )头(頭)上( )有( )许(許)多( )白( )色( )的( )毛( )。
    - Tā de tóu shàng yǒu xǔduō báisè de máo.
    - There are many white hairs on his head.
  - 猫(貓)的( )毛( )很( )柔( )软(軟)。
    - Māo de máo hěn róuruǎn.
    - The cat's hair is very soft.
  - 这(這)条(條)围(圍)巾( )是( )用( )羊( )毛( )制(製)成( )的( )。
    - Zhè tiáo wéijīn shì yòng yángmáo zhìchéng de.
    - This scarf is made of wool.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 毛](@media/glyph6bdb.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 匕
- **definition:** cane
- **pinyin:** bǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a spoon
  - **interpretation:** The character 匕(bǐ, 'cane') originally depicts a spoon, which has a similar shape to the character itself. It is unrelated to the meanings of 'walking cane', 'knife', or 'person', which appear in other characters with similar forms.
- **examples:**
  - 古( )时(時)候( )的( )老( )人( )常( )用( )匕( )支( )撑(撐)。
    - Gǔ shíhòu de lǎorén cháng yòng bǐ zhīchēng.
    - In ancient times, elders often used a cane for support.
  - 他( )拄( )着(著)匕( )，在( )公( )园(園)里(裏)散( )步( )。
    - Tā zhǔ zhe bǐ, zài gōngyuán lǐ sànbù.
    - He walked in the park with a cane.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 匕](@media/glyph5315.png)
### 老年 → 年
- **definition:** year; age
- **pinyin:** nián
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾(“wheat; grain”) + 人(“person”) as phonetic ->
    - originally “harvest” ->
    - later “year”
  - **interpretation:** The character 年 (nián, "year") originally depicted a harvest of grains, linking the concept of agricultural cycles with the passing of a year. Over time, the form evolved, retaining the semantic component 禾 (hé, "grain") and using 人 (rén, "person") for its phonetic sound in early stages, which later transformed into the current form through script evolution.
- **examples:**
  - 今年是兔年。
    - Jīnnián shì tùnián.
    - This year is the Year of the Rabbit.
  - 他( )今( )年( )二( )十( )岁(歲)。
    - Tā jīnnián èrshí suì.
    - He is twenty years old this year.
  - 五( )年( )后(後)我( )希( )望( )能( )去( )旅( )行( )。
    - Wǔ nián hòu wǒ xīwàng néng qù lǚxíng.
    - I hope to travel in five years.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 年](@media/glyph5e74.png)
### 老年 → 年 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收( )获(穫)的( )禾( )香( )弥(彌)漫( )在( )田( )野( )中( )。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民( )辛( )勤( )耕( )作( )，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春( )雨( )滋( )润(潤)了( )禾( )苗( )，预(預)示( )着(著)丰(豐)收( )。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
